# Operation Log

Chronological record of significant operations. Each entry is its own file under `log/`; this page is the reverse-chronological index. See [concepts/parallel-session-coordination.md](concepts/parallel-session-coordination.md) for why.

- [2026-05-21 — Legacy `habitatFeatureStore` full retirement](log/2026-05-21-atlas-habitatfeaturestore-retirement.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the soft-deprecation deferral from the [habitat-features unification ADR](decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-habitat-features-unification.md) now that the unification is complete through Slice 8-F. **Commit `c25d667d`** deletes the geometry-less `habitatFeatureStore` (123 lines; `persist` `ogden-habitat-features` + zundo `temporal`) and its last live consumer `FeatureInventoryPanel` (the A2 add/remove tally form); removes the `'habitatFeature'` `undoCoordinatorStore` registration (added in `a2a7c8b1`) + the `blob('ogden-habitat-features', …)` `syncManifest` entry; unmounts the panel `<section>` in `HabitatAllocationCard` (gauge untouched, now-unused `apiProjectId` dropped); and tidies the `habitatCommitments.ts` docstring (stale `FeatureInventoryPanel` "Used by" reference — selectors already read only `DesignElement`s). The unified `DesignElement` `'habitat'` path is now the single source of truth; A3 `BiodiversityMonitorCard` remains the surviving placed-commitment readout via `selectPlacedHabitatCommitments`. **No migration** — legacy records carry no geometry, so faithfully placing them would invent steward locations (covenant forbids); per steward decision the persisted data is throwaway test data and the inert `ogden-habitat-features` localStorage key is left for manual clearing (no one-shot cleanup shim). The economics `habitatFeature: ProgramSubtotal` cashflow field (same name, unrelated concept) is untouched. **Verification:** `tsc --noEmit` (8 GB heap) only pre-existing foreign errors, no dangling import; `vitest run src/features/biodiversity src/features/plan` 143/143 across 11 files; dead-import grep clean (two comment-only historical refs remain); `vite build` (8 GB heap) succeeds — bundler resolved all chunks (full `npm run build` is gated by pre-existing foreign `tsc` errors + OOM'd on default heap, so `vite build` run directly); covenant grep zero hits. **Rebase-storm:** a concurrent session's `f568fb42` swept the pre-staged deletions in and `6fb588fb` reverted them mid-flight; re-established + committed with explicit paths the moment verification passed per `feedback_commit_immediately_on_rebased_branches`. ADR: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-habitatfeaturestore-retirement]].
- [2026-05-21 — WIP reconciliation: half-landed P4.5 / width-aware companions](log/2026-05-21-wip-reconciliation.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Re-landed three half-landed features whose headline commits shipped but companion files were dropped by external rebases. **Group A1** (`c4e5ed6c`): P4.5 register auto-creates personal org in a `db.begin` tx + `defaultOrgId` on login/me + organizations `PATCH /:id` + shared `UpdateOrganizationInput` — and fixed the mock-DB enqueue sequences in `auth.test.ts`/`smoke.test.ts` that the plan wrongly assumed were already updated (proved by stash-and-compare: base 18/18, with-A1 6 fails; api suite now 680 pass). **Group A2** (`f568fb42`): `defaultOrgId` on `ApiAuthUser` + authStore + 2 consuming test fixtures — **fixes the broken web tsc** (committed consumers read a field the type lacked). **Recovery** (`6fb588fb`): A2 accidentally swept two pre-staged foreign deletions (FeatureInventoryPanel, habitatFeatureStore) because the `git status` "staged" filter matched only `M `, not `D `; restored both. **Group B** (`a30fbd8a`): width-aware BE-line store-side `widthM` passthrough (inline-edit half + types already committed). **Group C** already re-landed externally (`b5932b2d`). 8 pre-existing typecheck errors remain on the branch baseline (4 in this author's `SelectionFloater.test.tsx` from `55e803d1`, vitest-only verified — flagged for follow-up). 21-stash pile + live MP-preview check deferred.
- 2026-05-21 — Site-intel import/export dock CSS re-land (rebase recovery) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. An external rebase dropped the `ExportButton.module.css` + `ImportSiteIntelButton.module.css` half of the [import/export relocation slice](log/2026-05-21-site-intel-import-export-relocation.md) back to uncommitted while the panel-side `SiteIntelligencePanel` `headerActions` edit survived. Without these two files the relocated header buttons keep their old floating-dock positioning (`position: absolute; left: 64px`). Re-committed both: `.dock` → `position: relative; display: inline-flex; pointer-events: auto`, popover anchored `top: calc(100% + 8px); right: 0; z-index: 20`. No logic change — pure CSS recovery of already-documented work, per `commit_immediately_on_rebased_branches`.
- 2026-05-21 — SectorCompass HUD tilts with map pitch (3D) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Follow-up to the bearing-rotation slice (`abcefa01`). User feedback: "change the angle of the compass as well — if map view at a 3d 45 deg angle, so should the compass." Single-file change to `SectorCompassOverlay.tsx`: added a `pitch` state alongside the existing `bearing`, collapsed both reads into one `sync` handler subscribed to `rotate`/`rotateend`/`pitch`/`pitchend` (reads `map.getBearing()` + `map.getPitch()`), and swapped the wrapper transform to `perspective(420px) rotateX(${pitch}deg) rotateZ(${-bearing}deg)` with `transformStyle: preserve-3d`. The compass now lays back to match the tilted ground plane in the Plan terrain3d view while north still spins correctly *within* the tilted disc. The "Sector compass" label stays a sibling outside the transformed wrapper so it remains upright. No mount-site edits (map prop already threaded from the prior slice); `SectorCompassDiagram` SVG untouched. `apps/web` typecheck zero new errors (6 baseline unchanged). Live `perspective()` px + rotateX sign tunable in preview per the plan's sign-check note.
- [2026-05-21 — Atlas cashflow per-program tooltip primitive](log/2026-05-21-atlas-cashflow-tooltip-primitive.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. **Slice 8-F** of the 2026-05-21 unification. Closes the deferred "richer ARIA-grade tooltip primitive" bullet under the Slice 8-D-2 closure note in the ADR. `StewardshipProgramsCashflowCard.tsx` now wraps each non-Phase cell's value in a `BreakdownTrigger` that mounts the design-system `Tooltip` primitive (`role="tooltip"` + `aria-describedby` + keyboard-focusable `<span tabIndex={0}>` trigger). The four-line per-program breakdown (Cover-crop / Habitat / Agroforestry / Tree-planting) is now exposed to touch users and screen readers, not just desktop hover. `Td`'s `title?: string` prop dropped. Data model on `PhaseCashflowRow` is unchanged — refactor is render-only. Tests rewritten to assert `role="tooltip"` descendants + `span[tabindex="0"]` instead of `getAttribute('title')`. 6/6 green.
- [2026-05-21 — Atlas habitat-feature inline-popover host-tree picker](log/2026-05-21-atlas-habitat-host-tree-picker.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. **Slice 8-E** of the 2026-05-21 unification. Closes the deferred "bespoke per-kind inline popovers" bullet from the ADR. New `buildHabitatFeatureEditSchema` in `inlineEditSchemas.ts` emits per-kind fields (mountingHeightM, heightM, approxHeightM+cavityCount) plus a conditional `hostTreeFeatureId` select for the four mount-on-tree kinds (owl-box / raptor-perch / nest-box / snag). Empty-state renders a readonly helper option ("Place an oak / pine / apple / shrub point first.") so stewards discover the dependency rather than being silently denied. `PlanSelectionFloater` extends the count-chip-as-button pattern (already used for paddock edit) to habitat-category DesignElements. Save deep-patches `habitatMetadata` immutably; empty values collapse to undefined. Stewardship sovereignty preserved — the user names the host; no auto-inference. Tests: 8 new schema cases + 1 popover→store→seeder roundtrip case proving the picker write surfaces as `dependsOnAuto: ['tree__<id>']` on the next push.
- 2026-05-21 — SectorCompass HUD follows map bearing — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Follow-up to the north-indicator triangle slice (`68b340d6`). User feedback: "need compass to actually continue pointing the right way when map view is rotated." Added optional `map?: maplibregl.Map` prop to `SectorCompassOverlay`; threaded `map={map}` from all four mount sites (`ObserveLayout.tsx`, `PlanLayout.tsx`, `VisionLayoutCanvas.tsx`, `ActLayout.tsx` — every existing canvas render-prop already had the instance in scope). Inside the overlay, a `useEffect` subscribes to MapLibre's `rotate` + `rotateend` events and stores the current `map.getBearing()` in local state; the SVG is wrapped in a `<div>` that applies `transform: rotate(${-bearing}deg)` with an 80ms linear transition for sub-perceptible smoothing. CSS transform is GPU-accelerated so per-frame jank is negligible. Pure-SVG `SectorCompassDiagram` stays untouched — rotation is applied on the wrapper, not inside the SVG geometry. External rebase wiped working tree mid-session; per `commit_immediately_on_rebased_branches` memory rule re-applied + committed inside the same turn. `apps/web` typecheck zero new errors (6 baseline unchanged).
- 2026-05-21 — SectorCompass north indicator — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Micro-fix on user feedback "Sector Compass should include arrow/triangle/symbol pointing north." Added a gold (`#c4a265`) north-pointing triangle just outside the outer ring of `SectorCompassDiagram.tsx`, rendered after wind / solar / manual wedges so it sits on top. In compact mode (overlay HUD — labels suppressed) an additional bold "N" glyph is rendered above the triangle so orientation is legible without the cardinal-label band. Non-compact mode (slideup full diagram) keeps the triangle and relies on the existing R_LABEL "N" cardinal-spoke label. Pure-SVG addition; no new dependencies or data flow. `apps/web` typecheck zero new errors (6 baseline unchanged).
- [2026-05-21 — Width-aware line rendering for Observe built-environment lines](log/2026-05-21-atlas-line-width-aware-rendering.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Drawn linear BE features (driveway / fence / power-line / buried-utility) now render at widths reflecting real-world metres via a feature-property + kind-default fed `interpolate ['exponential', 2]` zoom→pixel paint expression with `max(floor, m × scale)` clamp so narrow kinds stay legible at low zoom. Four files touched: `packages/shared/src/builtEnvironment.ts` adds `widthM` to `ExistingMetadata`; `packages/shared/src/builtEnvironmentKinds.ts` adds frozen `LINE_KIND_DEFAULT_WIDTH_M` record (9 kinds — driveway 3.5 m, fence 0.1 m, power-line 0.2 m, buried-utility 0.3 m, hedgerow 2.0 m, path 0.8 m, road 4.0 m, swale 1.5 m, insectary-strip 1.2 m) + `getLineKindDefaultWidthM` helper; `packages/shared/src/builtEnvironmentProjection.ts` threads `widthM` through the 4 Observe line projections; `apps/web/src/v3/observe/components/layers/ObserveAnnotationLayers.tsx` applies `beLineWidthExpr(defaultM)` to the 4 line layers with `coalesce(['get','widthM'], defaultM)` fallback. **Plan-side scope (DesignElement linear kinds) re-landed in a second slice** — the first attempt was reverted by the linter, but on retry the linter *integrated* the edits (system reminders confirmed "intentional"): `66fd2103` (elementCatalog `defaultWidthM` on swale/path/road/hedgerow/insectary-strip), `8ff17011` (designElementsStore `widthM?`), `c1c2ef45` (DesignElementLayers width-aware paint + ObserveAnnotationLayers `beLineWidthExpr` signature fix for `noUncheckedIndexedAccess`). **Per-feature `widthM` inline-edit field also landed** (`ff8ad259`): added to the four V2 BE line builders in `inlineEditSchemas.ts` (power line 0.2 / buried utility 0.3 / fence 0.1 / driveway 3.5, persisting via `existing.widthM`) plus insectary-strip in `buildHabitatFeatureEditSchema` (persisting to DesignElement top-level `widthM`); empty/invalid clears the override → catalog default. Observe `annotationFieldSchemas.ts` deliberately untouched — its four field schemas write through the V1 facade (no `widthM`); the V2 builders already serve both Plan and Observe stages. Verification: shared + web tsc exit 0; web vitest baseline green; `buildHabitatFeatureEditSchema.test.ts` 8/8. Live in-browser visual confirmation deferred to the steward per the recorded Claude-Preview WebGL gotcha. **Inline-edit forms for the plain Plan line kinds also landed** (`b2450691`): generic `buildLineFeatureEditSchema` exposes a Width (m) + Label form for hedgerow/path/road (placeholder/title from `findElementSpec`, `widthM` → DesignElement top-level), surfaced via a `LINE_EDIT_KINDS` count-label button in `PlanSelectionFloater`; `buildLineFeatureEditSchema.test.ts` 6/6. Remaining followup: V1 BE-store passthrough (routed through V2 projection layer to avoid the linter revert).

- [2026-05-21 — Phase G smoke test: live Evidence panels post-alias-fix](log/2026-05-21-phase-g-evidence-panels-smoke-test.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the Phase G ratchet by exercising the promoted `@ogden/shared/evidence` selector layer through the live browser after the [alias hotfix](log/2026-05-21-phase-g-vite-alias-hotfix.md). Scope (user-confirmed): all three Evidence panels — `SiteSummaryNarrativeSection`, `DecisionTriad`, `LandVerdictCard` — desktop + mobile, fresh-account auth. **Live mount evidence (`SiteSummaryNarrativeSection`).** 1440×900, project `2662072f-0c7d-4bad-9203-ccdd9c35440c` (351 House — Atlas Sample; Three Streams Farm not accessible to the fresh account due to pre-existing sync 422). DecisionRail expanded; SiteIntelligencePanel rendered ("49 Overall Suitability · Data layers: 2/7"). One `evidence-toggle` labelled `"▸Show evidence (3)"`; after click, `evidence-body` visible with 3 `evidence-fragment` rows + 3 `evidence-source-pill`s; body text matched expected narrative shape. **Headline finding — IA gap, not a Phase G regression.** `apps/web/src/routes/index.tsx:139-149` redirects `/project/$projectId` unconditionally to `/v3/project/$projectId/observe`; neither `ProjectPage` nor `MobileProjectShell` are imported into the live route tree. `DecisionTriad` + `LandVerdictCard` are therefore unreachable through the live IA on this branch (consistent with the `7-stage lifecycle retiring` memory rule). Selectors are unit-tested green in `packages/shared/src/evidence/__tests__/selectors.test.ts` and resolve through the same alias just smoke-tested green in the live mount; source-level the import is identical, so runtime correctness for the two unreachable panels is inferred, not measured. **Network.** `POST /api/v1/projects/$id/evidence-audit/log` returns 404 — route not registered in the local `apps/api` build; `emitEvidenceAudit` swallows per its fire-and-forget contract at `auditEmit.ts:45`. Pre-existing infra gap, unrelated to the selector promotion. **Console** red-error-free for evidence code; only red line is the pre-existing sync 422. **Phase G ratchet — closed.** Module resolution holds (post-hotfix), selector dispatch returns a populated `EvidenceItem`, `EvidenceSection` renders every expected `data-testid`, `emitEvidenceAudit` fires as designed. **Deferred (not Phase G):** sync 422 on `GET /api/v1/projects`; missing `POST /evidence-audit/log` API route in local env; templates migration 034 not applied locally; `MobileProjectShell` mount route never re-introduced after the v3 IA cutover (either restore a route, surface the two panels inside `/v3`, or delete them + their selectors). **Lesson:** "panel rendered in tests" ≠ "panel reachable in IA" — Phase G's 1851-test vitest pass tells you the selectors and components both work; it does not tell you whether the live IA still mounts them. Future selector-promotion work should grep `apps/web/src/routes/` for live mount paths before declaring runtime parity.
- [2026-05-21 — Phase G hotfix: Vite alias for `@ogden/shared/evidence`](log/2026-05-21-phase-g-vite-alias-hotfix.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Unblocks dev-server boot after Phase G G.1 added `./evidence` to `packages/shared/package.json` exports but did not update the parallel `resolve.alias` map in `apps/web/vite.config.ts`. Symptom: Vite v6.4.1 returned HTTP 500 on `DecisionTriad.tsx` / `LandVerdictCard.tsx` / `auditEmit.ts` with "Failed to resolve import `@ogden/shared/evidence`"; React root never mounted. Root cause: `vite.config.ts:172-196` carries an explicit alias map for every `@ogden/shared/*` subpath because Vite's dev-server cwd is `apps/web/` and cannot traverse up to the workspace-root node_modules; the bare `@ogden/shared` entry prefix-matched any unaliased subpath and rewrote it to `packages/shared/src/index.ts/evidence` (nonsense). Node's resolver was happy (verified via `require.resolve`); Vite's alias-first chain short-circuited before reaching the exports field. Fix: one-line add at `apps/web/vite.config.ts:194` — `'@ogden/shared/evidence': resolve(__dirname, '../../packages/shared/src/evidence/index.ts')` — placed before the bare-package fallback per the "more-specific first" rule in the surrounding comment. Verification: all three modules HTTP 200; `apps/web` typecheck clean for evidence code (3 pre-existing unrelated errors untouched: `StepBoundary.tsx`, `HostUnionContextMenu.test.tsx`, `HostUnionDrilldownCard.test.tsx`). Lesson: future subpath additions to `packages/shared/package.json` exports **must also** add the matching `vite.config.ts` alias entry — the two surfaces are parallel and Vite's prefix-match silently fails for any apps/web consumer otherwise.
- [2026-05-21 — Phase G: server-side evidence-audit replay tool](log/2026-05-21-phase-g-evidence-audit-replay.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the F.4 deferred "server-side replay tool" follow-up; the Evidence ledger now has a read-back path. **G.1 (`f32c7c58`)** promotes all 8 selectors + `selectEvidenceFor` dispatcher + `hashInputs` + `types.ts` from `apps/web/src/lib/evidence/` to `packages/shared/src/evidence/`; new barrel re-exports the public surface plus `EthicKey` / `EthicStatus`; `./evidence` exports entry added to `packages/shared/package.json`; 10 apps/web consumers + `auditEmit.ts` redirected to `@ogden/shared/evidence`; selector self-imports rewritten to relative paths to avoid the package self-import circular. Shared tests now run in shared: **21 files / 318 tests passed** (incl. 41 selector + 8 hashInputs cases). **G.2 (`8f55a45b`)** new `apps/api/src/scripts/replayEvidenceAudit.ts` exports `replayEvidenceAuditSince(sql, sinceIso) → ReplayResult { totalRows, okRows, failRows, failures[] }`; per-row checks recompute `hashInputs(input_payload)` against `input_hash`, validate `panel_key` is in the 8-key dispatch set, then `stableStringify(selectEvidenceFor(...))` against the stored `evidence_output`; never throws on per-row mismatch. Thin CLI parses `--all-since <ISO>`, opens its own postgres pool, exit 0/1/2; `evidence:replay` pnpm script. **G.3 (`89cf2a5d`)** self-cleaning pgtest covering clean sweep + tampered `evidence_output` (`output-mismatch`) + corrupted `input_hash` (`hash-mismatch`); fixtures cover `land-verdict` + `three-ethics` + `capital-partner`; `resetDb` cascades audit rows; green-skips when Docker is absent. **G.4 (this commit)** ADR + log + index + LAUNCH-CHECKLIST strike. - [2026-05-21 — Click-delete vertex fix (onMouseUp → onClick)](log/2026-05-21-click-delete-vertex-fix.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Bug-fix for user-reported "clicking on a vertex does not remove it" in real Chrome. Root cause: `clickDeleteDirectSelect.ts` attached deletion to `onMouseUp`, but MapboxDraw's `events.mouseup` routes click-gestures (`isClick`: ≤ 4 px / ≤ 500 ms) to `currentMode.onClick`, drag-releases to `currentMode.onMouseUp` — so plain vertex clicks never reached the delete branch. Two slices: **`90fef60a`** moved deletion to `onClick`, dropped the now-redundant in-mode pixel-threshold (MapboxDraw's own `isClick` already gates), and returns early without delegating to `stock.onClick` when the min-vertex guard fires (otherwise `clickActiveFeature` clears `selectedCoordPaths` and kicks the user out of vertex-edit on the 3rd vertex of a triangle); also resets `_cdVertexCoordPath` on every `onMouseDown`. **`16dc2d79`** appended a corrective "later" section to the [partial smoke-walk log](log/2026-05-21-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete.md) striking through its "harness limitation" framing — the harness was a red herring layered on top of a real regression. Typecheck exit 0. Real-browser keystroke confirmation of the remaining smoke-walk steps still owed. Branch hygiene: stashed unrelated parallel-session edits (basemap-water-adoption + template_slug migration) before commit, restored after push; `git fetch` 2/0 before push; FF clean.

- [2026-05-21 — Observe-anno "stuck source" diagnosis closed as headless-RAF artefact](log/2026-05-21-observe-anno-sources-false-alarm.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. **No code change.** Wiki-only documentation closing the "four observe-anno sources never reach `loaded:true`" investigation as not-a-bug. Live preview verification at `/v3/project/mtc/observe` with two seeded Conventional Crop polygons shows `m.isSourceLoaded('observe-anno-conventional-crop') === true` and `queryRenderedFeatures` returning the crop with correct `annoKind`/`annoId` props — after exactly one `_render()` tick. The prior session's "render loop is dead" conclusion was a property-name miss: it probed `m._frame`, but MapLibre 5.x renamed that field to `_frameRequest` and now schedules frames via `AbortController` + `browser.frameAsync` ([`node_modules/maplibre-gl/dist/maplibre-gl-dev.js:57944`](../node_modules/maplibre-gl/dist/maplibre-gl-dev.js)). Re-probing the correct field shows a frame IS queued — it just never resolves while the Claude Preview tab is backgrounded (headless Chrome throttles RAF for inactive tabs). All geojson sources show the same idle-paused profile in the preview (`be-v2-*`, `matrix-*-dem`, `design-el-extrusion`, `diagnose-parcel-boundary`), not just the named four; the "siblings load normally" framing in the brief was a probe-timing artefact. **Diagnostic technique worth keeping:** when debugging "isSourceLoaded never true" under Claude Preview, force a paint via `m._render(performance.now())` from the eval console to drain `_updatedSources` and resume paused SourceCaches synchronously enough to read a real state. **Implication for the [vertex-edit + click-delete smoke walk](log/2026-05-21-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete.md):** if "clicks don't open detail panels" reproduces in a real browser, the cause is not stuck sources — likelier suspects are `SelectionFloater` consuming the click before the layer handler, the 50 ms `consumedAt` deduper in `ObserveAnnotationLayers.tsx` mis-rejecting, or the form store's `existingId === id && kind === kind` early-return. Disposition: closed as not-a-bug; future sessions should re-test in a real browser before re-opening this thread.

- [2026-05-21 — Observe matrix+patches model + Fill-remainder tool](log/2026-05-21-observe-matrix-patches-and-fill-remainder.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Single commit `2a6def92`. Vegetation + pasture now describe the ground-cover *matrix*; crops + buildings sit on top as opaque *patches* rather than translucent blends. Four phases in one slice: (1) `conventionalCrop` fill-opacity 0.22 → 0.55 and `building` 0.35 → 0.6 in `ObserveAnnotationLayers.tsx` so patches occlude the matrix underneath (layer-order already correct). (2) New pure `netCoverAreaM2(patches, subtractees)` in `earth-water-ecology/derivations.ts` — per-patch `turf.area − Σ turf.area(turf.intersect(patch, sub))`, clamped at zero, summed; wired into `ecologyDetailKpis` with subtractees = crops ∪ buildings; surfaces as a new "Ground cover (net)" KPI in `EcologicalDetail`. 5 new vitest cases pin empty/no-subtractees/enclosed/fully-covered/non-overlapping. `@turf/turf` v7 trap noted: `turf.intersect` takes a `FeatureCollection` of two polygons, not two positional `Feature` args. (3) `vegetationStore` + `pastureStore` geometry widened to `GeoJSON.Polygon | GeoJSON.MultiPolygon` so Fill-remainder can store disjoint pieces; `annotationGeometryRegistry.writePolygon` accepts the union with per-kind narrowing (hazard/building/septic/conventionalCrop early-return on MultiPolygon, vegetation/pasture accept both); `readPolygon` returns the union; `annotationFieldSchemas` vegetation/pasture save guards widened. MapboxDraw `direct_select` only handles single Polygons, so `AnnotationVertexEditHandler.readPolygon` adapter narrows to Polygon-only (returns `null` for MultiPolygon) — vertex-edit gracefully disables on those records, drag-reposition still works. MapLibre fill/line layers handle MultiPolygon natively, no paint change. (4) New **"Fill remainder (subtract crops & buildings)"** checkbox in `VegetationTool` and `PastureTool` popovers — when on, `place(boundary)` runs `subtractPatches`: reduce `turf.difference(turf.featureCollection([acc, turf.feature(g)]))` over crops ∪ buildings; `null` result (boundary fully covered) bails with a `console.info` and skips creation, otherwise the Polygon/MultiPolygon flows through the existing `createWithDefaults() → form → addPatch()` path. No new store API beyond the Phase 3 schema bump. **Verification.** `npx --no-install vitest run` (full apps/web) 1703/1703 across 173 files (+5 over the prior 1698). `npm run lint` (= `tsc --noEmit`) clean. DOM check at `/v3/project/mtc/observe`: both popovers render the checkbox. Screenshot tool unresponsive (map-tile blocking the renderer); flagged transparently per CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success." **Out of scope.** Snap-to-existing-edge, render-time masking, crop/raised-bed MultiPolygon, Plan-stage changes, toast UI on full-coverage bail, vertex-edit on MultiPolygon (intentionally disabled), DB / shared-package schema changes. **Branch governance.** Fetched + verified no divergence prior to commit per [[project-branch-rebase]]; committed the moment lint + tests cleared per [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]].

Two commits — round 1 `14db482f` adds an "Edit vertices" button to `AnnotationDetailPanel` (gated on `POLYGON_KINDS.has(kind) || LINESTRING_KINDS.has(kind)`; sector arcs and point kinds excluded), routing through `observeSelectionStore.set([{kind,id}]) + setMoveMode(true) + closeStore()` (NOT the local `close` wrapper — that clears selection) so the existing `AnnotationVertexEditHandler` path picks up. `conventionalCrop` and `pasture` registered in `POLYGON_KINDS` of `annotationGeometryRegistry` with new `readPolygon` / `writePolygon` cases routing to `useConventionalCropStore.updateConventionalCrop({ geometry })` + `usePastureStore.updatePasture({ geometry })`. Round 2 `bcd5e0ad` adds **click-to-delete vertex** via a new `clickDeleteDirectSelect.ts` custom MapboxDraw mode that spreads `MapboxDraw.modes.direct_select` and overrides four lifecycle methods: `onMouseDown` stashes cursor screen-point; `onVertex` captures `coord_path`; `onMidpoint` clears the capture (midpoint click adds a vertex — stock behaviour, must not delete the freshly-added one); `onMouseUp` arbitrates click-vs-drag via `Math.hypot(dx, dy) > CLICK_PIXEL_THRESHOLD` (4 px). Click on vertex with capture intact → `feature.removeCoordinate(path)` + `map.fire('draw.update', { features: [feature.toGeoJSON()] })`, which `SharedVertexEditHandler.onUpdate` already consumes — no persistence changes. Min-vertex guard `canRemoveCoordinate(feature, coordPath)`: polygons require `ring.length > 4` (closed-ring triangle = 4 entries), lines require `coords.length > 2`. Silent refusal per user choice — no toast. `SharedVertexEditHandler.tsx` registers the mode on the per-mount `MapboxDraw` instance and switches `changeMode` from `'direct_select'` to `CLICK_DELETE_DIRECT_SELECT`; Plan-stage `PlanVertexEditHandler` inherits for free via composition. **Behaviour.** Click vertex (no drag) → vertex deleted; click+drag → moves (unchanged); midpoint click → adds vertex (unchanged); click vertex on triangle / 2-vertex line → nothing (silently gated); Esc → exits vertex-edit (unchanged); Cmd-Z → restores via store `temporal()` middleware. `draw_polygon` mode for new polygons unaffected. **Verification.** `pnpm --filter @ogden/web typecheck` shows only 3 pre-existing unrelated errors (`StepBoundary.tsx:365`, two `HostUnion…` test files) — none in touched files. Interactive smoke test **not run** — API at `localhost:3001` offline (ECONNREFUSED), blocked login on Vite preview; flagged transparently per CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success." **Out of scope.** Bulk vertex delete (shift-click multi-select); toast on min-vertex refusal; click-delete on points (no vertices, repositioned via `AnnotationDragHandler`); sector arc click-delete (uses `AnnotationSectorHandles`, not vertex-edit). ADR: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-observe-vertex-edit-and-click-delete]]. Behavioural memory: [[feedback-commit-immediately-on-rebased-branches]] (both slices committed the moment typecheck cleared); [[project-branch-rebase]] (fetched + verified no divergence prior to commit).

- [2026-05-30 — B4 tooltip multi-pin (Slice L)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-multi-pin.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice L of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap. Retires the 2026-05-26 single-pin invariant: `pinnedUnion` (single `{ point, entries, hostIds }` object) replaced with `pinnedHosts: Map<string, HostBlock>` keyed by hostId; per-host click toggle, ESC + tap-outside clear ALL pins, single cursor-anchored stack merging pinned (insertion order, `pinned: true`) with hover (filtered by `!pinnedHosts.has`, `pinned: false`). `lastCursorPointRef` freezes the anchor when the cursor leaves canvas with pins active. Gold accent moves from container-level `.tooltip[data-pinned='true']` (border-color) to per-block `.hostBlock[data-pinned='true']` (2px gold left-border + 6px padding-left) so mixed pinned + hover stacks distinguish sticky from hover-along blocks at a glance. `HostBlockEntry` gains `pinned: boolean` (kept off `HostBlockProps` so the raw-data interface stays narrow); scroll-cap derivation moves from `!!pinned` to `entries.some(e => e.pinned)`. `sameHostIdSet()` helper deleted. **Use-case justification.** Roadmap required "design conversation about whether the use case (steward wanting to compare 2+ hosts side-by-side) is real before committing." Consulted **Permaculture Scholar NotebookLM (`5aa3dcf3-…`)** — unequivocal yes, citing four canonical permaculture design flows requiring simultaneous comparison of overlapping host canopies: (1) **50-year mature-canopy simulation** (spacing for tree A depends on B/C/D's mature spreads in the same frame); (2) **Edge maximization** (Holmgren P11 "Use Edges and Value the Marginal" — biodiversity concentrates in spaces *between* canopies; productive edge can't be designed one tree at a time); (3) **Cross-guild ecological aggregation** (N-fixers + dynamic accumulators + insectaries aggregate into coverage or redundancy — multi-guild question by definition); (4) **Suntrap / microclimate engineering** (U-shape / horseshoe arrangements creating sheltered microclimates — aggregate footprint + continuous shadow evaluated as a unit). Holmgren P8 ("Integrate Rather Than Segregate") underwrites all four. Single-pin was a segregation affordance working against P8. Scholar citations degenerate (~290 references to same handful of snippets — known indexer artifact); substantive claims hold independently against any permaculture-design textbook. **Key architectural choices.** `Map<hostId, HostBlock>` for O(1) per-host toggle + insertion-order iteration (newly-pinned at top of pinned section, consistent with 2026-05-27 topmost-first convention). Per-block accent not container-level so mixed stacks communicate sticky vs hover-along visually. `pinned` on `HostBlockEntry` not `HostBlockProps` (display-state, not raw-data payload). Single cursor-anchored stack rather than separate portals per pin (matches "these are the hosts I'm comparing" mental model). ESC + tap-outside clear ALL pins per roadmap recommendation ("get this off my screen" rarely scoped to one host). In-tooltip dismiss button OUT OF SCOPE — below Slice K's threshold=4 the tooltip is `pointer-events: none`, can't receive clicks without retiring the 2026-05-25 invariant; Slice M's drill-down surface (interactive by design) can ship it. **Tests.** Migrated test #3 from container-level `pinned` prop to per-entry; scroll-cap tests migrated to entry-level `pinned: true`. New `describe('multi-pin (Slice L)', ...)` with four cases: mixed pinned + hover (only pinned blocks carry data-pinned; root never carries data-pinned), all-pinned stack (every block carries data-pinned; separators between), all-hover stack (no data-pinned anywhere), scrollable regression guard (1 pinned + 3 hover = 4 ≥ threshold ⇒ scrollable because `entries.some` predicate, guarding against future tightening to "all pinned"). **Verification.** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers` → 28/28 (24 prior + 4 new). `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 288/288 (36 files; +4 over Slice N's 284). `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files; pre-existing unrelated errors elsewhere unchanged. Preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree (Vite resolves against worktree-root `node_modules` which doesn't exist) — stated explicitly per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success." **Invariants preserved.** Slice K scroll-cap carve-out + tooltip-testid tap-outside exemption; Slice J / I / H; 2026-05-25 `pointer-events: none` in hover mode + pinned-small-stack; 2026-05-27 multi-feature fan-out (each feature toggles independently); 2026-05-28 ESC + tap-outside dismiss (semantics flip from "clear one" to "clear all"); 2026-05-29 / 30 fade machinery (`pinned` rides alongside `phase`); 2026-05-30 Slice N i18n seam (no new strings). **Invariant retired.** 2026-05-26 single-pin explicitly rolled back; ADR remains in wiki as historical context (defensive reasoning correct at the time, design question now answered). **Out of scope.** In-tooltip dismiss button (Slice M's space); pinned-count badge ("📌 N" header indicator — additive, defer); per-guild breakdown line inside a block (Slice O rejection deferred this to Slice M); persistence across page reloads (transient UI); keyboard navigation between pinned blocks (accessibility pass); integration tests for `PlanDataLayers` click-toggle Map logic (defer until a regression points at it). Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N + O + L shipped. **Remaining: Slice M** (hover-card drill-down — per-block click opens a richer surface listing per-guild breakdowns; depends on L's per-block addressability, which now exists).
- [2026-05-30 — B4 per-layer tinted stripe rejection (Slice O — second pass)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-per-layer-stripe-rejection.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice O of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap as a **documentation-only rejection** — no code change. The roadmap was explicit that this slice "must start with a research/decision step … decide whether the stripe is genuinely distinguishable (different surface) or re-introduces the same problem (same concept, different shape). Only then design the implementation, or document the second rejection with fresh reasoning." This slice ships the second-rejection path. **Prior rejections recap.** 2026-05-24 halo viz ADR colored the union halo neutral grey, explicitly rejecting `LAYER_TINT`: *"Neutral grey (not LAYER_TINT) because the union is a per-host aggregate, not a per-layer geometry; layer-tinting would mislead the eye into reading the halo as canopy-layer-specific."* 2026-05-25 hover tooltip ADR carried the reasoning forward to the tooltip stripe: *"the union is a per-host aggregate; layer-tinting would reintroduce the misleading-hue concern 2026-05-24 called out for the halo itself."* Both deferred as "revisit if needed." **Fresh counter-argument considered.** The natural revisit: the halo is on the map (color = layer-data), but the tooltip is a *separate UI surface* with its own visual conventions (already carries a gold "saved overlap" accent — a non-data color), so a stripe there would read as "category metadata," not as "this geometry = green-layer." **Why the counter-argument fails on two grounds.** (1) **Visual contiguity.** The tooltip is cursor-anchored adjacent to the halo it describes — stewards see them simultaneously. A green stripe next to a grey halo invites the eye to bind "this host = green," propagating the layer-tint association from the *label* onto the halo it labels. The surface boundary doesn't exist for the eye when the surfaces are positionally adjacent; the 2026-05-24 reasoning survives unchanged: the stripe tints the halo's label, which is the same problem one frame downstream. (2) **"Dominant" is the wrong reduction.** A host is in the silvopasture data because it carries *multiple* canopy layers (polyculture by construction). Every available definition of "dominant" elevates one layer above the others — biggest area biases toward fast-spreading shrubs, most members biases toward groundcovers, tallest requires schema work (data model doesn't track per-member heights), alphabetical is arbitrary and defensible only as a tie-breaker. Polyculture composition is the load-bearing feature of the model; hiding four-fifths of it behind one layer's color is a model violation, not a presentation choice. **What the steward actually needs (and where it goes).** The existing counts line — *"3 guilds · 7 canopy-bearing members"* — already surfaces polyculture composition. If at-a-glance per-layer breakdown matters, the right UI is a small list inside the tooltip (e.g. `overstory ×2 · midstory ×3 · understory ×2`), with each layer name in its own tint *as a label, not as a category color for the host as a whole*. **This breakdown is not in scope for Slice O** — it overlaps with **Slice M** (hover-card drill-down), where the natural design move is to expand a block into a richer surface that lists per-guild breakdowns. Whoever picks Slice M up next can lean on this ADR's reasoning to justify the breakdown approach. **Status flip.** 2026-05-24 / 25 ADRs left this as "deferred — revisit if needed." This slice flips it to **decided rejection**. Future roadmap sweeps should not re-list it as candidate work without the underlying constraint (silvopasture is polyculture-by-construction; "dominant layer" is information loss) materially changing. **Out of scope.** Code changes (none, by design); per-guild breakdown line in the tooltip text (Slice M's space); layer-aware *icons* on the tooltip (canopy/midstory/understory glyphs — distinct from color-tint, worth a separate design conversation); changes to the existing `LAYER_TINT` palette on the map's per-member geometries (those remain correct — per-member geometries genuinely belong to a single layer); light/dark theming (separate deferral). **Verification.** No code change → no tests to run, no tsc to check, no preview-server to verify. The slice's deliverable is this log entry + the ADR; both are reviewable in `git log`. **Invariants preserved.** Every B4 invariant from earlier ADRs holds verbatim — no surface has been touched. Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N shipped as code; **O shipped as a documented rejection**. Remaining: **Slice L** (multi-pin — substantial slice; needs design conversation about whether the "steward wants to compare 2+ hosts side-by-side" use case is real before committing) and **Slice M** (hover-card drill-down — depends on L's per-block addressability).
- [2026-05-30 — B4 tooltip i18n seam (Slice N)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-i18n-seam.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice N of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap by shipping the small-path option (path 2): extracts every English string the tooltip surfaces into a new colocated `tooltipStrings.ts` module with a clean seam for future i18next adoption, **without** bootstrapping i18next project-wide. **What changed.** New `apps/web/src/v3/plan/layers/tooltipStrings.ts`: `tooltipStrings` const object holds 3 row labels (`unionFootprint` = "Union footprint", `rawDiskSum` = "Raw π·r² sum", `savedOverlap` = "Saved overlap"); two formatter functions encapsulate the unit-suffix + pluralization logic — `formatAreaM2(n)` rounds + appends " m²", `formatHostCounts(guildCount, memberCount)` renders the counts line with English n===1 binary pluralization ("guild"/"guilds", "member"/"members"), the " · " separator, and the "canopy-bearing" qualifier all baked in. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` removes its inline `formatM2` helper, imports the three exports, swaps inline ternaries for the formatter call, and replaces bare string literals with `{tooltipStrings.unionFootprint}` etc. 6 formatter unit tests pin area rounding (incl. 0.49 → "0 m²" toward-zero edge) + plural/singular/zero-as-plural combinations. **Why path 2 not path 1.** `react-i18next` + `i18next` are deps but **zero** `useTranslation` / `i18n.init` call sites exist anywhere in `apps/web/src` — the tooltip would be the first consumer. Path 1 would force five ADR-worthy decisions in this slice's scope: bootstrap location, `<I18nextProvider>` wrapper near the app root (startup-time + pending Atlas-portal SSR consideration), resource-file layout (namespace boundaries), bundle-size assessment (~30kB gzipped naively bundled), and a project-wide copy-migration policy. The constants module gets the strings *organised* without forcing any of those bets; path 1 stays available as a follow-up when a second locale is confirmed. **Why a TS module, not a JSON resource file.** JSON is standard i18next layout but can't hold the formatter functions — splitting them now would leave a half-organised seam. When i18next lands, formatters become a thin shim around `t()` and the string-constant object migrates to JSON; the file shrinks or disappears. **Why keep English n===1 in-module.** A real i18n library will replace it with CLDR plural rules per locale (Arabic: six forms; Russian: three). Current formatter signature `(count, count) => string` is narrow on purpose — future swap to `t('tooltip.hostCounts', { guildCount, memberCount })` requires no call-site changes. **Migration recipe documented** in the module header docstring: (1) add `apps/web/src/i18n/index.ts` i18next bootstrap, (2) wrap `<App />` in `<I18nextProvider>`, (3) swap `tooltipStrings.foo` for `t('tooltip.foo')`, (4) move values into `locales/en/tooltip.json`, (5) delete the module. **Strings preserved byte-identically.** Row labels, " m²" suffix, " · " separator, "canopy-bearing" qualifier, n===1 binary pluralization — all unchanged. The existing tooltip rendering tests pass without modification, strong evidence the refactor changed nothing observable. **Verification.** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers` → 24/24 (12 tooltip + 6 memberDragMath + 6 new tooltipStrings); `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 284/284 (36 files; +6 over Slice K); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files; preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success" — refactor is a pure extraction whose visible output is byte-identical per the unchanged rendering tests. **Invariants preserved.** All Slice K (scroll-cap carve-out, data-scrollable threshold=4), J / I / H, and earlier B4 invariants (mouseleave-driven dismiss in hover mode + small-pinned, single-pin, multi-feature fan-out, touch tap-outside dismiss, enter + exit + per-block + reverse-in-flight fade, `prefers-reduced-motion`). **Out of scope.** Bootstrapping i18next (path 1, deferred); extracting strings from any other surface (tooltip-only by scope); number formatting beyond m² (decimal separators, grouping — available once i18next lands); RTL layout (separate infrastructure decision — CSS logical properties + `[dir]` attribute on `<html>`). Roadmap status: H + I + J + K + N shipped; next is **Slice O** (per-layer tinted accent stripe — research/decision step first, may ship as a "still rejected" ADR rather than code) per the approved execution order.
- [2026-05-30 — B4 tooltip max-height scroll cap (Slice K)](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-scroll-cap.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice K of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap — the highest-risk wave-C entry because **any** scroll affordance on the host-canopy-union tooltip requires `pointer-events: auto`, which collides with the 2026-05-25 invariant that the tooltip must NEVER steal the underlying union layer's mouseleave. **The carve-out.** `.tooltip[data-scrollable='true']` activates only when `pinned=true AND entries.length >= 4`. The CSS rule adds `max-height: calc(100vh - 80px)`, `overflow-y: auto`, and `pointer-events: auto`. Below either condition the invariant survives verbatim: hover mode + any host count = `pointer-events: none` and mouseleave-driven dismiss; pinned + 1–3 hosts = same. Above both conditions, mouseleave is moot — when pinned, dismissal is via ESC, click-again-on-host, or tap-outside-canvas-and-outside-tooltip, none of which depend on the tooltip's pointer-events. **Tap-outside handler carve-out (PlanDataLayers).** `onDocPointerDown` would have dismissed pointerdowns on the tooltip's scrollbar/content (target not in canvas → fall through). New early-return: `if (target instanceof Element && target.closest('[data-testid="host-canopy-union-tooltip"]')) return;`. The tooltip is portalled to the document body so PlanDataLayers can't hold a ref to it — the data-testid already used by tests becomes the production query selector, no portal-aware ref forwarding needed. **Edge-clamp adjustment.** Raw `entries.length * PER_BLOCK_H` would over-reserve vertical space when the surface is scroll-capped (e.g. 20-host pinned stack) and push the anchor unnecessarily high; new `scrollCapMaxH = Math.max(PER_BLOCK_H, viewportH - 80)` bounds the estimatedH when `scrollable`. `Math.max(PER_BLOCK_H, ...)` guards against pathologically short viewports. **Threshold = 4.** Three hosts (~340px) fits 768px viewport comfortably; four (~448px) tight; five+ clips. Single `SCROLL_CAP_THRESHOLD = 4` module constant so a future tuning round can move it without touching consumers. **Reserve = 80px.** `calc(100vh - 80px)` matches the existing edge-clamp's intuitive budget (12px cursor gap + 8px padding at top/bottom + DesignToolRail headroom); on a 720px viewport ~640px usable ≈ 5.9 blocks, "scroll if you must" not "scroll constantly." **Why not WAAPI / wheel-capture.** The roadmap's alternative — capture `wheel` events on the document, translate to a CSS-variable offset on a virtual scrollable container — would preserve the 2026-05-25 invariant verbatim but re-implement overscroll, inertia, scrollbar-drag, keyboard scroll, and require a separate `touchmove` path for tablets. The dual carve-out (CSS + tap-outside) ships in ~10 lines and inherits every native scroll affordance for free; the narrow carve-out window keeps the invariant holding in every state the steward meets during normal hover flow. **Why threshold-by-entry-count not viewport-bound.** The cleaner predicate would be `scrollable = pinned && rawEstimatedH > scrollCapMaxH`, but (a) entries.length is stable across viewport changes (resize doesn't toggle the carve-out under a pinned steward) and (b) the test surface stays simpler. If the fixed threshold proves wrong for small viewports, swap the predicate without changing the data-attribute contract. **Reused, not built:** existing portal mount; existing data-testid; existing tap-outside listener; existing edge-clamp logic; existing fade machinery (data-visible / data-exiting / transition tokens). **Tests added:** 4 under `scroll-cap carve-out (Slice K)` describe — below-threshold pinned = no data-scrollable; above-threshold unpinned = no data-scrollable (hover invariant survives); at-threshold pinned = data-scrollable='true'; very-tall (20-host) pinned at viewport-top = data-scrollable='true' + edge-clamp produces non-negative top (regression guard). **Verification:** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan/layers/__tests__/HostCanopyUnionTooltip.test.tsx` → 12/12 (8 prior + 4 new); `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 278/278 (35 files; +4 over Slice J); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on the three touched files (pre-existing unrelated errors elsewhere unchanged); preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success" — data-attribute contract fully unit-test-covered, visible scroll relies on browser-native `overflow-y: auto`. **Invariants preserved:** 2026-05-25 (mouseleave-driven dismiss in hover mode + pinned-small-stack), 2026-05-26 (single-pin), 2026-05-27 (multi-feature fan-out), 2026-05-28 (touch tap-outside dismiss), 2026-05-29 + 30 (enter + exit + per-block + reverse-in-flight fade), `prefers-reduced-motion`. **Out of scope:** Slice L multi-pin (separate slice; depends on this one), Slice M hover-card drill-down (depends on L), viewport-aware predicate, sticky block headers when scrolling, keyboard arrow-key navigation between blocks. Roadmap status: H + I + J + K shipped; next is **Slice N** (tooltip i18n small path) per the approved execution order.
- [2026-05-30 — B4 InlineFeaturePopover exit fade (Slice J)](log/2026-05-30-b4-inline-popover-exit-fade.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice J of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap, consuming the `--motion-overlay-*` tokens added in Slice I. Click-driven inline mini-form `InlineFeaturePopover` adopts the same deferred-unmount machinery the 2026-05-30 host-canopy-union tooltip ship landed: a `displayed: InlineFormPayload | null` mirror state lives one exit-transition longer than `useInlineFormStore.active`, `exiting: boolean` flips at the same time `active` goes null, `visible: boolean` flips via `useLayoutEffect` after mount so the enter transition fires from `opacity: 0`/`translateY(2px)` → `opacity: 1`/`translateY(0)`. CSS-Module `.popover` rule gains the from-state + `transition: opacity var(--motion-overlay-duration) var(--motion-overlay-ease-out), transform var(--motion-overlay-duration) var(--motion-overlay-ease-out)`. New `.popover[data-visible='true']` selector targets the visible state; new `.popover[data-exiting='true']` mirrors the from-state, switches the easing token to `--motion-overlay-ease-in`, and adds **`pointer-events: none`** so a mid-fade click on a fading Save/Cancel button is physically impossible. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` block nulls both transitions so reduced-motion users see instant dismissal. **The interactivity invariant difference from the tooltip.** Tooltip is `pointer-events: none` — invariant: "must never steal events from the underlying layer." Popover is `pointer-events: auto` — owns inputs, Save, Cancel, custom actions. So the tooltip's invariant doesn't transfer. New invariant: **a mid-fade click on a fading button must not race the displayed-mirror cleanup.** Defense-in-depth: exit-state CSS drops `pointer-events: none` (primary defence), Save/Cancel handlers also guard on `if (!active)` (free insurance — store entry has cleared by the time exit starts). **Value-reset block now skips active=null.** Pre-fade logic unconditionally cleared `values` when `active` went null; with deferred unmount the form renders through the fade and clearing values mid-fade would visually empty every input. New logic only resets when active becomes a **new non-null payload**; active going null is the exit signal and values stay frozen until `displayed` clears. **`onPopoverTransitionEnd` filters on three conditions.** `propertyName === 'opacity'` (rejects the transform-property transitionend so the unmount is deterministic and tied to the visually-disappearing property), `target === currentTarget` (rejects bubbled child transitionends from nested `<input>`, `<select>`, `<button>` focus-ring + hover-state transitions), `exiting === true` (rejects post-reverse-in-flight transitionends that would spuriously unmount a restored form). 200ms safety `setTimeout` covers `prefers-reduced-motion` where transitionend never fires. **Render guard switched from `if (!active) return null` → `if (!displayed) return null`** so the form stays mounted through the fade; title, fields, customActions iteration all read from `displayed`. New 4-test suite `InlineFeaturePopover.test.tsx` pins: cold-start renders nothing; `open()` mounts with `data-visible='true'`; `close()` flips `data-exiting='true'`, transform-property transitionend does NOT unmount but opacity-property transitionend does; reverse-in-flight `open()` during exit restores form and subsequent opacity transitionend does not spuriously unmount. Uses the same `fireTransitionEnd(el, propertyName)` `Object.defineProperty` happy-dom helper as the 2026-05-30 tooltip tests. **Reused, not built:** Slice I `--motion-overlay-*` tokens; deferred-unmount pattern from the 2026-05-30 tooltip ship; existing ESC + click-outside listeners (still gated on `active` so they auto-detach at exit start — correct, because the form is no longer interactive). **Invariants preserved:** schema-driven render (title, fields, customActions, required-field gate, disclosure expansion) unchanged; ESC + click-outside dismiss; reduced-motion behaviour. **Out of scope:** the slide-up dialog used for written reports (different surface class — slide-up animation, not fade); cubic-bezier alignment of overlay surfaces with the project's `--ease-out`/`--ease-in` family (deferred per the Slice I ADR; revisit when a third consumer arrives); per-field exit animations within the popover. **Verification:** `npx vitest run src/v3/plan src/features/agroforestry` → 274/274 green (35 files; +4 new InlineFeaturePopover tests; 8/8 tooltip tests untouched); `npx tsc --noEmit` clean on touched files (pre-existing unrelated errors in `LandAssessmentSlideUp.tsx`, `AtlasAIPanel.tsx`, `HydrologyRightPanel.tsx` confirmed unchanged via baseline grep); preview-server visual check not possible in this worktree (Vite resolves against worktree-root `node_modules` which doesn't exist) — stated explicitly per project CLAUDE.md "say so rather than assuming success," structurally identical to the 2026-05-30 tooltip ship whose contract is fully unit-test-covered. Roadmap status: H + I + J shipped; next is **Slice K** (max-height scroll cap when N hosts is large) which carries the `pointer-events` carve-out risk.
- [2026-05-30 — B4 motion-token harmonisation (Slice I)](log/2026-05-30-b4-motion-token-harmonisation.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes Slice I of the B4 tooltip remaining-deferrals roadmap. Extracts the four hard-coded overlay-fade literals from `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.module.css` (duration `120ms`, translate `2px`, easing `ease-out`/`ease-in`) into a new `--motion-overlay-*` token family declared on `:root` in [apps/web/src/styles/tokens.css](../apps/web/src/styles/tokens.css) alongside the existing `--duration-*` / `--ease-*` families. Four sites of `transition: opacity 120ms ease-... , transform 120ms ease-...` rewritten as `var(...)` calls; three `translateY(2px)` sites likewise. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` block unchanged (nulls `transition` entirely, no per-token override needed). **Why a new family, not reuse `--duration-*` / `--ease-*`.** Existing duration ladder is 100/200/400/600ms; tooltip's 120ms was tuned because 100ms felt snappy and 200ms felt draggy under cursor motion. Existing `--ease-out`/`--ease-in` are cubic-beziers (`cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)` / `cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)`); tooltip ships with bare CSS keywords (`cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.58, 1)` / `cubic-bezier(0.42, 0, 1, 1)`). Coercing to either would ship a visual change as part of a "token extraction" slice. New family preserves literals verbatim; cubic-bezier alignment deferred to a follow-up ADR after Slice J's adoption verifies the current curves feel right with two consumers. **Why CSS custom properties, not TS constants.** CSS Modules can't reference TS without inline `style={{}}` (loses scoping) or a CSS-in-JS pipeline (overkill for four literals). The 200ms safety timeout in `PlanDataLayers.tsx` does duplicate `--motion-overlay-duration + slack`, but the slack is the load-bearing part — if a second JS consumer materialises we'll revisit. **Why these four tokens specifically.** Two easings (not one) because enter accelerates toward the visible state and exit decelerates away from it; CSS variables can't carry direction. One duration (not three) because the 2026-05-30 ship uses 120ms across enter / exit / reverse-in-flight — different durations per intent would be a design change, not extraction. **Tokens.css is already imported once at the app root via [app/index.css:6](../apps/web/src/app/index.css), so no additional wiring needed and CSS custom properties propagate through the cascade into CSS-Modules-scoped class names.** Tests untouched — contract tests only assert data-attrs + event handling, neither affected by value extraction. 8/8 tooltip + 63/63 agroforestry green. Touched files TS-clean. **Unlocks Slice J** (InlineFeaturePopover exit fade) which can adopt the same tokens at birth so the two map-overlay surfaces fade in sync. Roadmap deferrals: cubic-bezier alignment, dark-mode-only overrides, additional surface-class families (`--motion-modal-*` etc) all kept deferred.

- [2026-05-30 — B4 follow-up: per-block tooltip fade + reverse-in-flight](log/2026-05-30-b4-tooltip-perblock-fade-and-reverse.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the last two still-deferred bullets from the 2026-05-29 exit-fade ADR: per-block exit fade in multi-host stacks, and reverse-in-flight animation when `activeUnion` returns non-null mid-exit. Fade machinery refactored from CSS keyframes (`@keyframes tooltipFadeIn` / `tooltipFadeOut`) to **CSS transitions** on opacity + transform; `.tooltip` mounts at `opacity: 0` and `.tooltip[data-visible='true']` flips to `opacity: 1` (the enter transition fires from a `useLayoutEffect` that sets `visible=true` on mount); `.tooltip[data-exiting='true']` takes opacity back to 0 with `ease-in` timing. New `.hostBlock` rule mirrors the same shape for per-block fades. `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce` override nulls all four selectors' `transition`. **Reverse-in-flight is free** with transitions: removing `data-exiting` mid-fade lets the transition interpolate from the current visible value back to 1, with no snap and no JS — making the 2026-05-29 monotonic-key remount pattern unnecessary. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` exports a new `HostBlockEntry` interface (hostId + per-entry `phase: 'entering' | 'exiting'`); `HostBlock` renders `data-testid='host-block-${hostId}'`, `data-exiting='true'` when phase==='exiting', and an `onTransitionEnd` filtered by `propertyName==='opacity'` + `target===currentTarget` that fires a new `onEntryExited?: (hostId: string) => void` prop. Container's own `onTransitionEnd` filters by both `propertyName==='opacity'` and `target===currentTarget` so bubbled per-block transitionends don't fire `onExited`. **Merge-by-hostId.** `PlanDataLayers.displayedUnion` state shape replaces 2026-05-29's `key + entries: HostBlock[]` with per-entry phase tracking (`entries: HostBlockEntry[]`); the monotonic key is gone. The mirror `useEffect` rewrites the merge: kept hosts (in both old and new sets) carry forward with phase `entering` and refreshed data; dropped hosts (in old but not new) flip to phase `exiting` and stay in the array; new hosts are appended in MapLibre topmost-first order. The React `key` on the rendered map iterator is now `entry.hostId` (stable per host) so a block's in-flight transition isn't cancelled when siblings drop out and the array re-indexes. `onEntryExited` callback drops the hostId from the entries array — or clears the mirror entirely if the last block just finished fading. Safety timeout bumped 180 → 200 ms (120 ms transition + 80 ms slack to absorb event-loop jitter and the `prefers-reduced-motion` instant-change case where transitionend doesn't fire). **Test scaffolding.** New `fireTransitionEnd(el, propertyName)` helper — `@testing-library/dom`'s `createEvent.transitionEnd` passes init to the constructor without a fallback, and happy-dom's `TransitionEvent` constructor silently drops the `propertyName` init key, so the helper `Object.defineProperty`'s the value onto the event post-construction. Existing tests migrated from `fireEvent.animationEnd({ animationName: 'tooltipFadeOut' })` to the new helper. Two new tests: reverse-in-flight asserts that flipping `exiting` from true → false during re-render clears `data-exiting` and a subsequent opacity transitionend does NOT fire `onExited`; per-block exit asserts that an entry with `phase='exiting'` carries `data-exiting='true'`, that opacity transitionend fires `onEntryExited(hostId)`, and that sibling `entering` blocks + transform-property transitionends do not. **Why transitions, not WAAPI.** The 2026-05-29 ADR speculated about `element.animate()` + `animation.reverse()`. Transitions get the same behaviour with zero JS: they always interpolate from the current computed value, which is exactly what "reverse" means for a single-property fade. **Why merge by hostId.** When the active set shrinks, the dropped host has to stay in the displayed array long enough to fade; indices shift under set changes, so a key-by-index would cancel its transition when the array re-reconciled. Invariants preserved: `pointer-events: none`, single-pin model, ESC + tap-outside-to-dismiss, multi-feature fan-out (2026-05-27), edge-clamp + entries-aware `ESTIMATED_H` (counts every block including phase-`exiting` ones so a tooltip about to lose a block stays clamped conservatively — no flicker-reposition mid-fade), reduced-motion behaviour (was: no keyframe animation; now: no transition). 71/71 vitest green (8 tooltip + 63 agroforestry; +2 tooltip tests over the 2026-05-29 ship). Touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-29 ADR reverse-in-flight + per-block bullets flipped open → closed.

- [2026-05-21 — fix(web): Vite dev proxy translates ECONNREFUSED into API_OFFLINE envelope](log/2026-05-21-vite-proxy-api-offline-envelope.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the "Response not JSON (500)" papercut on `POST /api/v1/auth/register` from `http://localhost:5200/login`. Confirmed via `Test-NetConnection` + direct `/health` probe that nothing was listening on port 3001; the 500 was Vite's dev proxy returning plain-text HTML for `ECONNREFUSED`, not the API (whose global `setErrorHandler` in `apps/api/src/app.ts` *always* sends a JSON envelope, so a non-JSON 500 cannot originate there). Added `configure` + `proxy.on('error', …)` to the `/api` entry in `apps/web/vite.config.ts` that emits a `503` carrying the API's own envelope shape `{ data: null, error: { code: 'API_OFFLINE', message: "API server unreachable at http://localhost:3001 (<errno>). Start it with:  pnpm --filter @ogden/api dev" } }`. `apiClient.ts` flows the envelope through unchanged → LoginPage `role="alert"` banner renders the actionable instruction verbatim. Iterated once on the message format — first draft wrapped the command in backticks; when an operator pasted the banner verbatim into PowerShell, the backticks parsed as line-continuation and `(ECONNREFUSED)` as a sub-expression call. Plain-text form is copy-paste safe. Verified in live preview: API stopped → in-page `fetch('/api/v1/auth/register')` returned `503` + envelope, LoginPage banner DOM matched verbatim, console error stream flipped from `ApiError: Response not JSON (500)` to `ApiError: API server unreachable …` at the moment Vite picked up the config change; API restarted → same call returned `201` + `{ token, user }`. No edits to auth routes (`apps/api/src/routes/auth/index.ts` was sound), no new migrations, no dev seed-user script (explicitly declined — permanent fix only). ADR: [[decisions/2026-05-21-atlas-vite-proxy-api-offline-envelope]].

B. 6 project_layers with `source_api` strings sourced verbatim from the canon Observe-module → adapter mapping (NRCan HRDEM, OMAFRA CanSIS, OHN, Conservation Halton O.Reg. 162/06, AAFC ACI, ECCC normals via Georgetown WWTP) — elevation + climate use the 018 canonical snake_case key set, remaining four use 017 camelCase shape; C. terrain_analysis (rolling 4–8 % slope band, South dominant aspect, mixed N/E secondary); D. site_assessment with `score_breakdown` JSONB reflecting Y2 state (overall 68.0, FAO S2, USDA Class III, confidence medium); E. ~22 design_features (Y0 baseline fields, Y1 keyline swales + riparian buffers + cover-crop blocks, Y2 orchard + pasture + poultry + nursery + kitchen garden + pole barn + egg-pack room + cistern + farm lanes + hedgerows, Y3+ silvopasture savanna + woodlot extension planned); F. 2 spiritual_zones (musalla at central tributary creek confluence with `qibla_bearing 55.85°`, gathering circle near homestead); G. 8 project_relationships edges (Needs & Yields integration graph — livestock manure → orchard fertility; cover crop → soil OM; riparian buffer → baseflow → pasture; hedgerow → pollinator habitat; ponds → microclimate; propagation tunnel → planting pipeline; keyline swales → infiltration). `030_three_streams_regeneration_trajectory.sql` lands 24 `regeneration_events` on MDPI Apricot Lane Y0/5/9 cadence — 6 Y0 (2024) baseline observations (soil OM %, bird-species richness, earthworm counts/m², infiltration mm/hr, pollinator visitation /10 min, water-retention capacity); 8 Y1 (2025) events (keyline swales + riparian buffers as interventions, Q2 worm-cast count, oats + radish cover crop, winter rye + crimson clover cover crop, Q4 infiltration spot-check, spring bird survey, Y1-close milestone); 10 Y2 (2026) events through current (pole barn + cistern milestone, orchard block planted, cow-calf herd arrival, mobile poultry online, second-round MDPI sampling, trajectory reflection); `phase` field maps to the `regeneration_events` CHECK vocabulary (`stabilize_erosion` / `improve_drainage` / `build_organic_matter` / `introduce_perennials`); calendar-year tag carried in `observations.cohortYear` JSONB key. Trajectory deltas baked in: cropped-field OM 1.65 → 2.25 % (+36 %), bird-species richness 11 → 17 (+55 %), cropped-field earthworms 0.8 → 4.6 / m² (+475 %), cropped-field infiltration 11.8 → 24.8 mm/hr (+110 %), pollinator visitation 5 → 23 / 10 min (+360 %). Does four things in order: 1. Customises the 4 default phases (Year 0-1 / Water + Cover, Year 1-3 / Perennials + Livestock, Year 3-5 / Polyculture Maturation, Year 5+ / Ecosystem Stability) via `phaseStore.ensureDefaults(pid)` + per-phase `updatePhase`; 2. Sets Site Profile facets to canon (180 acres, climate zone 5b, rolling, 5.8 % avg slope, currentLandCover `'cropland'`, high soil compaction, rainfed water posture, frost dates 05-15 / 10-05, household {2 adults, 2 children}); 3. Runs `seedGoalCompassPlan(pid)` so the engine path generates canon-grounded WorkItems byte-identical to a real UI generation; 4. Adds 6 nursery propagation batches (hawthorn whips, elderberry cuttings, serviceberry from seed, winter rye + crimson clover seed stock, kitchen-garden transplants). **Auto-run hook** uses a side-effect import in `main.tsx` registering a one-shot `useProjectStore.subscribe` listener that fires on first project-in-store hit + unsubscribes itself — avoids editing the WIP `projectStore.ts` modified file, removes circular-import question entirely. New shared constant `THREE_STREAMS_PROJECT_ID = '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000357320'` in `packages/shared/src/constants/system.ts`, re-exported via existing `system.js` export line. **Decisions fixed this phase:** Two migrations not four (followed 017 comprehensive precedent over plan's 018–021 split); migration numbering reassigned to 029 + 030 (plan slots taken); no habitat-feature / ecology / cover-crop-window client seed (out of scope per task list); no featured landing-page treatment (Task 2.6 skipped per plan; Phase 3 portal CTAs will deep-link); B-track livestock substrate deferred to Phase 2.5 per plan; wired auto-run via subscription not direct projectStore edit (zero circular-import risk). **Reused, not built:** 017 migration pattern (Section A-I template, `ON CONFLICT (id) DO NOTHING` on pinned sentinels), 018 canonical snake_case layer-key set for elevation + climate, 015 regeneration_events CHECK-constraint vocabulary, `seedGoalCompassPlan` engine path (runs real sequencing + spine push), `phaseStore.ensureDefaults` 4-phase scaffold, `siteProfileStore.setFacet` real per-facet setters, `nurseryStore.addBatch` per-row idempotent add, `is_builtin=true` auto-surfacing in `/projects/builtins` + `/v3/project`, `seedBuiltinObserveData` auto-run pattern (mirrored alongside, not edited), `__ogden*` debug-handle convention. **Out of scope per plan:** Phase 2.5 livestock substrate; Phase 3 portal; Phase 4 template; live adapter re-fetch (vendored `summary_data` per 017); MDPI Y5/Y9 forward projections (Phase 3 portal scenes); habitat features + ecology + planting-calendar cover-crop windows (Phase 2.5 follow-up); refactor of WIP `projectStore.ts` (zero edits needed). **Verification:** `apps/web` `tsc --noEmit` (with `--max-old-space-size=8192`) clean on all touched files; only error remains the pre-existing `StepBoundary.tsx(365,7)` `unknown → ReactNode` foreign-WIP baseline. - [2026-05-29 — B4 follow-up: tooltip exit fade](log/2026-05-29-b4-tooltip-exit-fade.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes the last fade-related still-deferred bullet from the 2026-05-25 host-union-hover-tooltip ADR (deferred again on 2026-05-28): animated fade **out**. `PlanDataLayers.tsx` gets a third `useState` (`displayedUnion`) that mirrors `activeUnion = pinnedUnion ?? hoveredUnion` but lives one exit-animation longer, with `phase: 'entering' | 'exiting'` and a monotonic `key`. A `useEffect([activeUnion])` writes the mirror synchronously on non-null `activeUnion` (fresh `key` remounts the tooltip so the enter keyframe replays — covers re-enter during in-flight exit) and flips the mirror's phase to `'exiting'` on null `activeUnion`. A 180 ms safety `setTimeout` (120 ms anim + 60 ms slack) covers the `prefers-reduced-motion` short-circuit case where `animationend` never fires. Portal-render now reads `displayedUnion`, forwards `key`, `exiting`, and `onExited`, and forces `pinned={false}` during exit so the gold accent doesn't linger. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.tsx` props extended with optional `exiting?` + `onExited?`; root `<div>` gets conditional `data-exiting='true'` and an `onAnimationEnd` handler that fires `onExited()` when `exiting === true` and `animationName.includes('tooltipFadeOut')` (CSS Modules scopes the keyframe name; `.includes` matches the scoped form). `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.module.css` adds `@keyframes tooltipFadeOut` (opacity 1→0, translateY 0→2px — the reverse of the enter keyframe); `.tooltip[data-exiting='true'] { animation: tooltipFadeOut 120ms ease-in forwards; }` — `forwards` holds the final state until React unmount. The `prefers-reduced-motion` media block extended to null both keyframes. New test asserts `data-exiting` forwarding + `onExited` fires on `tooltipFadeOut` animationend and NOT on unrelated keyframe names. Why not `useRef` or `useReducer`: refs don't trigger re-render (the portal-branch needs to subscribe); two-shape state machine doesn't justify reducer boilerplate. Why force `pinned=false` during exit: gold accent reads "sticky," fade reads "going away" — stacking confuses the surface. Invariants preserved: `pointer-events: none`, single-pin, single-tooltip, multi-feature fan-out, edge-clamp, enter fade, tap-outside dismiss. 69/69 vitest green (6 tooltip + 63 agroforestry). Touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-25 + 2026-05-28 ADR exit-fade bullets flipped to closed.
- [2026-05-28 — B4 follow-up: tooltip touch tap-outside dismiss + enter fade](log/2026-05-28-b4-tooltip-touch-dismiss-and-fade.md) — **Branch.** `feat/atlas-permaculture`. Closes two still-deferred bullets from the 2026-05-25 host-union-hover-tooltip ADR: touch-device tap-to-show (the real gap was tap-outside-to-dismiss; show was already covered by MapLibre's synthesised `click` from the 2026-05-26 pin handler) and animated fade in/out (enter half — exit fade still deferred). `PlanDataLayers.tsx` host-canopy-union `useEffect` gets a new `onDocPointerDown` listener registered on `document` next to the existing ESC `onKey`: while `pinnedUnion` is set, a `pointerdown` whose target is outside `map.getCanvasContainer()` calls `setPinnedUnion(null)`. Taps *inside* the canvas still flow through MapLibre's existing `click` handler — 2026-05-27 set-equality toggle + replace semantics untouched. Pointer Events unify mouse + touch; `pointerdown` fires before `click` so outside taps dismiss before any other handler runs. `HostCanopyUnionTooltip.module.css` adds `@keyframes tooltipFadeIn` (opacity 0→1 + translateY 2px→0); `.tooltip` gets `animation: tooltipFadeIn 120ms ease-out`; `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)` override nulls it so reduced-motion users see the prior snap-in. CSS-only — no React state, no animation library. Why not `touchstart` on the layer: pinning side already works on touch via synthesised `click`; only dismissal needs new wiring. Why not exit fade: would require keeping the portal mounted past `activeUnion → null` (deferred-unmount state) — purely cosmetic, separate slice if needed. Invariants preserved: `pointer-events: none` on the tooltip (new listener is on `document`, not the tooltip), single-pin model, ESC desktop unpin, multi-feature fan-out semantics, `entries.length`-aware edge-clamp. No test changes — CSS animations don't run in happy-dom and the touch listener lives below this file's mock surface; existing 5 tooltip + 63 agroforestry tests remain green. Touched files TS-clean. 2026-05-25 ADR's touch tap-to-show bullet fully flipped open → closed; animated fade enter half flipped, exit half kept deferred.
